[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Stress at work with 7 questions:

**Stress at Work Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We are interested in understanding the stress levels and experiences of our employees at work. Your responses will help us identify areas where we can improve and provide a better work environment. Please answer the questions honestly and to the best of your ability.

**1. How often do you feel stressed at work?**

a) Almost never
b) Rarely
c) Sometimes
d) Often
e) Almost always

**2. What are the most common sources of stress at work for you? (Select all that apply)**

a) Meeting deadlines
b) Lack of control over tasks
c) Conflicting priorities
d) Unfair workload
e) Lack of communication from management
f) Other (please specify)

**3. How do you typically cope with stress at work?**

a) Take a break and do something relaxing
b) Talk to a colleague or supervisor about my concerns
c) Try to push through and focus on the task at hand
d) Take a few deep breaths and try to calm down
e) Other (please specify)

**4. Have you experienced any physical symptoms of stress at work (e.g. headaches, fatigue, muscle tension)?**

a) Yes, frequently
b) Yes, occasionally
c) No, never

**5. Do you feel like your workload is manageable and reasonable?**

a) Yes, I have a good balance of tasks
b) Mostly, but some days are more challenging than others
c) No, I often feel overwhelmed

**6. How confident do you feel in your ability to manage stress at work?**

a) Very confident
b) Somewhat confident
c) Not very confident
d) Not at all confident

**7. Are there any changes or initiatives that you think would help reduce stress at work? (Open-ended question)**

Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us understand and address stress at work.

Here is a questionnaire on Workplace Environment with 7 questions:

**Workplace Environment Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We value your opinion and would like to understand your perceptions about our workplace environment. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more comfortable and productive work space for everyone.

**1. How would you rate the overall comfort and cleanliness of your workspace?**

a) Very comfortable and clean
b) Somewhat comfortable and clean
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat uncomfortable and dirty
e) Very uncomfortable and dirty

**2. Do you feel that your workspace is well-lit and free from distractions?**

a) Yes, it's perfect
b) Mostly, but there's room for improvement
c) Neutral
d) Mostly, but there are some distractions
e) No, it's not ideal

**3. How would you rate the noise level in your workspace?**

a) Quiet and peaceful
b) Moderate, with some background noise
c) Loud and distracting
d) Varies depending on the time of day
e) Other (please specify)

**4. Are you satisfied with the temperature and air quality in your workspace?**

a) Yes, it's just right
b) Mostly, but there's room for improvement
c) Neutral
d) Mostly, but it's too hot/cold
e) No, it's not comfortable

**5. Do you feel that your workspace is organized and easy to navigate?**

a) Yes, it's very organized
b) Mostly, but there's some clutter
c) Neutral
d) Mostly, but it's hard to find things
e) No, it's disorganized

**6. How would you rate the availability and quality of amenities such as break rooms, restrooms, and parking?**

a) Excellent, they're well-maintained and convenient
b) Good, with some room for improvement
c) Neutral
d) Fair, with some issues
e) Poor, they need significant improvement

**7. Are there any specific changes you would like to see made to improve the workplace environment?**

(Open-ended question for respondents to provide their suggestions)

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Remote working experience with 10 questions:

**Remote Working Experience Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We value your feedback and would like to understand your experiences and opinions on remote working. Your responses will help us improve our remote working policies and practices.

**1. How often do you currently work remotely?**

a) Daily
b) Several times a week
c) Occasionally
d) Rarely

**2. What are the most significant benefits you've experienced while working remotely? (Select all that apply)**

a) Increased productivity
b) Better work-life balance
c) Reduced commuting time
d) Improved focus
e) Other (please specify)

**3. What are the biggest challenges you've faced while working remotely? (Select all that apply)**

a) Difficulty separating work and personal life
b) Limited access to company resources or tools
c) Feeling disconnected from colleagues and team
d) Difficulty staying motivated and engaged
e) Other (please specify)

**4. How do you currently stay connected with your team and colleagues while working remotely?**

a) Regular video meetings
b) Email and instant messaging
c) Phone calls and voicemails
d) Virtual collaboration tools (e.g., Slack, Trello)
e) Other (please specify)

**5. What do you think is the most important aspect of a successful remote working experience?**

a) Clear communication and expectations
b) Access to necessary resources and tools
c) Flexibility and autonomy
d) Regular feedback and check-ins
e) Other (please specify)

**6. Have you experienced any difficulties with work-life balance while working remotely? If so, how do you manage it?**

a) Yes, by setting clear boundaries and schedules
b) Yes, by prioritizing self-care and personal activities
c) No, I don't experience difficulties with work-life balance
d) Other (please specify)

**7. How do you currently prioritize your tasks and manage your time while working remotely?**

a) Using project management tools (e.g., Trello, Asana)
b) Creating a daily or weekly schedule
c) Prioritizing tasks based on importance and deadlines
d) Other (please specify)

**8. What do you think is the biggest misconception about remote working?**

a) That it's only for people who are self-motivated
b) That it's only for people who are introverted
c) That it's only for people who have a dedicated workspace
d) Other (please specify)

**9. Have you experienced any difficulties with technology or software while working remotely? If so, how did you resolve the issue?**

a) Yes, by seeking technical support from IT
b) Yes, by troubleshooting and finding a solution on my own
c) No, I don't experience difficulties with technology or software
d) Other (please specify)

**10. What do you think would improve your remote working experience?**

a) Improved communication and collaboration tools
b) More flexible work arrangements
c) Increased access to company resources and tools
d) Other (please specify)

Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and experiences with us!

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on End of Working Relationship with 10 questions:

**End of Working Relationship Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** This questionnaire aims to gather information about your experience when a working relationship comes to an end. Your responses will help us understand the process and identify areas for improvement.

**1. How would you rate the overall experience of ending a working relationship at our company?**

(Scale: 1 - Very Poor, 2 - Poor, 3 - Neutral, 4 - Good, 5 - Excellent)

**2. What was the primary reason for the end of the working relationship (e.g., job elimination, transfer, resignation, termination)?**

(Open-ended text response)

**3. Were you involved in the decision-making process regarding the end of the working relationship? If so, how involved were you?**

(Scale: 1 - Not at all, 2 - Somewhat, 3 - Moderately, 4 - Very, 5 - Extremely)

**4. Did you receive adequate support and resources during the transition period?**

(Scale: 1 - Strongly Disagree, 2 - Somewhat Disagree, 3 - Neutral, 4 - Somewhat Agree, 5 - Strongly Agree)

**5. How would you rate the communication from your manager/supervisor regarding the end of the working relationship?**

(Scale: 1 - Very Poor, 2 - Poor, 3 - Neutral, 4 - Good, 5 - Excellent)

**6. Were you satisfied with the outcome of the exit process (e.g., severance package, outplacement assistance)?**

(Scale: 1 - Very Dissatisfied, 2 - Dissatisfied, 3 - Neutral, 4 - Satisfied, 5 - Very Satisfied)

**7. Did you experience any challenges or difficulties during the end of the working relationship? If so, please describe.**

(Open-ended text response)

**8. How would you rate the overall fairness and transparency of the end of the working relationship process?**

(Scale: 1 - Very Poor, 2 - Poor, 3 - Neutral, 4 - Good, 5 - Excellent)

**9. Would you recommend our company's process for ending a working relationship to others? Why or why not?**

(Open-ended text response)

**10. Do you have any suggestions for improving the end of working relationship process at our company?**

(Open-ended text response)

Thank you for taking the time to provide your feedback! Your input is invaluable in helping us improve our processes.

a) Frequently (at least once a quarter)
b) Occasionally (about once a year)
c) Rarely (less than once a year)
d) Never

**2. What motivates you to participate in training sessions? (Select all that apply)**

a) To improve my skills and knowledge

e) Other (please specify)

**4. How would you rate the relevance of our training programs to your job responsibilities?**

a) Very relevant
b) Somewhat relevant
c) Not very relevant
d) Not at all relevant

**6. What do you think is the most valuable aspect of our training programs? (Select all that apply)**

b) Networking opportunities with colleagues and peers
c) Access to industry experts and thought leaders
d) Opportunities for professional certification or recognition
e) Other (please specify)

**7. How do you typically apply what you learn from training sessions in your daily work?**

a) Immediately, by implementing new skills and knowledge
b) Gradually, by incorporating new skills and knowledge over time
c) Rarely, as I often forget or don't have the opportunity to apply what I've learned
d) Not at all, as I don't see the value in applying what I've learned

**8. Have you ever experienced any barriers or challenges while participating in training sessions? If so, please describe.**

**10. Are there any specific topics or areas of training that you would like to see more emphasis on in the future?**

**11. Would you be interested in participating in a mentorship program or having a dedicated coach to support your professional development?**

a) Yes
b) No
c) Undecided

**12. Any additional comments or suggestions you'd like to share about our training programs?**

Here is a questionnaire on Career Development with 14 questions:

**Career Development Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We are interested in understanding your thoughts and experiences regarding your career development within our organization. Your feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and create opportunities for growth and development.

**Section 1: Career Goals and Aspirations**

1. What are your short-term career goals (next 1-2 years)? Please describe your aspirations and what you hope to achieve.

2. What are your long-term career goals (next 5-10 years)? How do you envision your career evolving within our organization?

**Section 2: Current Job Satisfaction**

3. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current job role and responsibilities?

4. What aspects of your current job do you enjoy the most? Please describe.

5. What aspects of your current job do you find most challenging? Please describe.

**Section 3: Learning and Development**

6. What skills or knowledge do you think are essential for your career growth and development?

7. How do you prefer to learn new skills or knowledge (e.g., training sessions, online courses, mentorship, etc.)?

8. Have you participated in any training or development programs within our organization? If so, what was your experience like?

**Section 4: Career Advancement and Opportunities**

9. What opportunities or challenges do you see for career advancement within our organization?

10. Are there any specific roles or departments you are interested in exploring for future career opportunities?

11. Do you feel supported in your career development by your supervisor or HR department? Please describe.

**Section 5: Feedback and Suggestions**

12. What do you think our organization could do better to support your career development?

13. Are there any specific resources or tools you would like to see available for career development (e.g., mentorship programs, career coaching, etc.)?

14. Is there anything else you would like to share about your career development or any suggestions you have for our organization?

Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your feedback is invaluable to us.

Please let me know if you'd like me to convert this into a specific format (e.g., Google Forms, Excel, etc.)!

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Career Path Clarity with 10 questions:

**Career Path Clarity Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We want to understand your perceptions of career path clarity within our organization. Your feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more transparent and supportive environment for career growth.

**1. How often do you feel uncertain about your career path within the company?**

a) Frequently
b) Occasionally
c) Rarely
d) Never

**2. When considering a new role or promotion, what factors do you rely on to make an informed decision? (Select all that apply)**

a) Job description and responsibilities
b) Salary and benefits
c) Company culture and values
d) Mentorship and support from superiors
e) Other (please specify)

**3. How important is it for you to have a clear understanding of the skills and qualifications required for your current role?**

a) Very important
b) Somewhat important
c) Not very important
d) Not at all important

**4. Have you ever felt stuck or unsure about your career progression within the company? If so, what steps did you take to address the issue?**

(Open-ended question for respondents to share their experiences)

**5. How would you rate the quality of feedback you receive from your supervisor or manager regarding your performance and career development?**

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor

**6. Do you feel that your current role aligns with your long-term career goals?**

a) Yes
b) No
c) Somewhat
d) Undecided

**7. How often do you discuss your career goals and aspirations with your supervisor or manager?**

a) Regularly (at least quarterly)
b) Occasionally (every 6-12 months)
c) Rarely (less than once a year)
d) Never

**8. What would you like to see changed or improved in terms of career path clarity within the company?**

(Open-ended question for respondents to share their suggestions)

**9. How confident do you feel in your ability to navigate the company's career development opportunities and resources?**

a) Very confident
b) Somewhat confident
c) Not very confident
d) Not at all confident

**10. Would you recommend our company as a place to grow and develop your career? Why or why not?**

(Open-ended question for respondents to share their opinions)

I hope this questionnaire helps you gather valuable insights on career path clarity within your organization!

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Career Path Clarity with 7 questions:

**Career Path Clarity Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We are interested in understanding your perceptions of career path clarity within our organization. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and develop strategies to support your career growth.

**1. How clear are you about the career paths available within our organization?**

a) Very clear - I have a good understanding of the different career paths and opportunities for advancement.
b) Somewhat clear - I have a general idea of the career paths, but could use more information.
c) Not very clear - I'm not sure what career paths are available or how to progress in my current role.
d) Not at all clear - I feel uncertain about my career prospects and opportunities for growth.

**2. Have you experienced any surprises or unexpected changes in your career path within our organization?**

a) Yes, I've experienced some surprises, but they've been minor and manageable.
b) Yes, I've experienced some significant surprises, and it's taken me time to adjust.
c) No, my career path has been relatively stable and predictable.
d) No, I've never experienced any surprises or changes in my career path.

**3. How important is it for you to have a clear understanding of your career path and opportunities for advancement?**

a) Very important - it's crucial for my job satisfaction and career growth.
b) Somewhat important - it's nice to have a clear understanding, but it's not essential.
c) Not very important - I'm more focused on my current role and responsibilities.
d) Not at all important - I don't think about my career path or opportunities for advancement.

**4. Have you received adequate support and guidance from your manager or HR department to help you navigate your career path?**

a) Yes, I've received excellent support and guidance.
b) Yes, I've received good support and guidance, but there's room for improvement.
c) No, I've received limited or no support and guidance.
d) No, I've never received any support or guidance.

**5. How often do you discuss your career goals and aspirations with your manager or HR department?**

a) Frequently - we discuss my career goals and aspirations regularly.
b) Occasionally - we discuss my career goals and aspirations every now and then.
c) Rarely - we rarely discuss my career goals and aspirations.
d) Never - we've never discussed my career goals and aspirations.

**6. Do you feel that your current role aligns with your long-term career goals and aspirations?**

a) Yes, my current role aligns perfectly with my long-term goals.
b) Yes, my current role is a good fit, but there's room for growth and development.
c) No, my current role doesn't align well with my long-term goals.
d) No, my current role is not aligned with my long-term goals.

**7. What would you like to see changed or improved to increase career path clarity within our organization?**

(Open-ended text field for respondents to provide their suggestions and feedback)

Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your input is invaluable in helping us understand your perspectives on career path clarity.

a) Daily/Weekly
b) Monthly
c) Quarterly
d) Rarely/Seldom

a) Yes, I have the skills and training I need
b) Mostly, I have some gaps but I'm working on filling them

d) Unsure

d) Not at all important - I'm not interested in career advancement

d) Other (please specify)

b) Limited opportunities for growth and development
c) Conflicting priorities and responsibilities
d) Other (please specify)

a) I prioritize my time and energy based on short-term goals and deadlines

**Introduction:** We are committed to providing a safe and healthy work environment for all employees. Please answer the following questions honestly, and your responses will be kept confidential.

**Question 1:** How would you rate the overall health and safety culture within our organization?

a) Excellent - I feel safe and supported at all times
b) Good - I generally feel safe, but there's room for improvement
c) Fair - I'm neutral about the health and safety culture
d) Poor - I don't feel safe or supported

**Question 2:** Have you ever experienced a near-miss or close call while working at our organization? If yes, please describe the incident and what you think could have been done to prevent it.

**Question 3:** How often do you feel that health and safety protocols are being followed and enforced by your supervisors and colleagues?

a) Always - I never see anyone compromising on health and safety
b) Most of the time - There may be occasional lapses, but overall, protocols are followed
c) Sometimes - I've seen some instances where protocols were not followed
d) Rarely - I rarely see health and safety protocols being followed

* Emotional intelligence

* Being transparent about goals and expectations
* Showing genuine interest in team members' lives and interests
* Demonstrating a sense of humor and approachability
* Other (please specify)

* Delegating tasks effectively
* Building and maintaining a strong team
* Staying up-to-date with industry trends
* Other (please specify)

**5.** How do you think leaders can best support the growth and development of their team members? (Select all that apply)

* Offering opportunities for training and development
* Encouraging innovation and experimentation

* Other (please specify)

**6.** What qualities do you think are essential for a leader to possess in order to effectively navigate change and uncertainty? (Select all that apply)

* Resilience
* Strategic thinking
* Emotional intelligence
* Other (please specify)

**7.** How would you rate the overall effectiveness of our organization's leadership in terms of driving results and achieving goals? (Scale: 1 = Not effective at all, 5 = Very effective)

b) Good - generally provides clear and timely communication, but may need improvement in some areas

d) Poor - does not provide clear, timely, or transparent communication, and may be unclear or inconsistent

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on Onboarding Experience with 8 questions:

**Onboarding Experience Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We value your feedback in helping us improve our onboarding process. Your responses will help us understand what we're doing well and what we can improve on. Please answer honestly, and feel free to provide additional comments or suggestions.

**1. How would you rate your overall onboarding experience?**

a) Excellent - I felt well-prepared and supported throughout the process.
b) Good - I had a positive experience, but there were some areas for improvement.
c) Fair - The onboarding process was average, and I didn't have any major issues.
d) Poor - I struggled during the onboarding process, and it took me a while to get up to speed.

**2. Which of the following best describes your first impression of our company culture?**

a) I felt immediately at ease and comfortable with the company's values and norms.
b) I was neutral - I didn't have a strong positive or negative impression.
c) I was a bit surprised or taken aback by the company culture.
d) I didn't get a strong sense of the company culture during onboarding.

**3. How effective was our onboarding program in providing you with the necessary information and resources to perform your job duties?**

a) Very effective - I felt well-equipped to start working independently.
b) Somewhat effective - I had most of the information I needed, but some things took me a while to figure out.
c) Not very effective - I had to rely on colleagues or search for information on my own.
d) Not at all effective - I felt lost and unsure about how to do my job.

**4. Were you satisfied with the frequency and quality of check-ins and feedback from your supervisor or HR during the onboarding process?**

Note that I used TYPE_ID 3 for questions 1, 4, and 5, which corresponds to the "Rating" question type. For question 2, I used TYPE_ID 1, which corresponds to the "Single Select" question type. For question 3, I used TYPE_ID 4, which corresponds to the "Open-ended" question type.

**WorkLife Balance Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We're interested in understanding how you manage your work and personal life. Your responses will help us identify areas where we can improve our company's support for WorkLife Balance.

**1. How often do you feel overwhelmed by work-related tasks and responsibilities, causing you to neglect your personal life?**

a) Frequently
b) Occasionally
c) Rarely
d) Never

**2. What are the most common activities you do outside of work to relax and recharge? (Select all that apply)**

a) Exercise/Sports
b) Reading/Hobbies
c) Spending time with family/friends
d) Traveling
e) Other (please specify)

**3. How many hours do you typically work outside of regular working hours (e.g., evenings, weekends)?**

a) Less than 1 hour
b) 1-2 hours
c) 2-4 hours
d) 4-6 hours
e) More than 6 hours

**4. Do you feel that your company provides adequate support for WorkLife Balance?**

a) Strongly agree
b) Somewhat agree
c) Neither agree nor disagree
d) Somewhat disagree
e) Strongly disagree

**5. What would you like to see changed or improved in our company's policies or practices to better support WorkLife Balance?**

(Open-ended text field for respondents to provide their suggestions)

**6. How important is WorkLife Balance to you, and do you feel that it affects your job satisfaction?**

a) Very important - it affects my job satisfaction
b) Somewhat important - it affects my job satisfaction
c) Not very important - it does not affect my job satisfaction
d) Not at all important - it does not affect my job satisfaction

[LLM ANSWER]
Here is a questionnaire on WorkLife Balance with 7 questions:

**WorkLife Balance Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We are interested in understanding your experiences and perceptions about WorkLife Balance at our company. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and develop strategies to support your overall well-being.

**1. How often do you feel overwhelmed by work demands, leaving you little time for personal activities?**

a) Frequently (more than 3 times a week)
b) Occasionally (1-2 times a week)
c) Rarely (less than 1 time a week)
d) Never

**2. How do you typically spend your free time outside of work hours? (Select all that apply)**

a) Relaxing and unwinding (e.g., reading, watching TV)
b) Pursuing hobbies or interests (e.g., sports, music, art)
c) Spending time with family and friends
d) Running errands or doing chores
e) Other (please specify)

**3. Do you feel that your work schedule allows for sufficient time for personal and family responsibilities?**

a) Yes, my schedule is well-balanced
b) Mostly, but there's room for improvement
c) No, my schedule is too demanding
d) It depends on the specific project or deadline

**4. How important is it for you to have a clear separation between work and personal life?**

a) Very important - it's essential for my well-being
b) Somewhat important - it's nice to have a break
c) Not very important - I'm comfortable blending work and personal life
d) Not at all important - I don't see a difference

**5. Have you experienced any negative impacts on your personal life due to work-related stress or demands? (Select all that apply)**

a) Increased anxiety or stress
b) Decreased motivation or energy
c) Changes in sleep patterns or appetite
d) Strained relationships with family or friends
e) Other (please specify)

**6. What would you like to see changed or improved to achieve a better WorkLife Balance at our company?**

(Open-ended text response)

**7. How confident are you that your manager and colleagues understand and support your WorkLife Balance needs?**

a) Very confident
b) Somewhat confident
c) Not very confident
d) Not at all confident

Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us create a more supportive and balanced work environment.

c) Rarely

Here is a questionnaire on WorkLife Balance with 7 questions:

**WorkLife Balance Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We value your input in understanding the challenges and opportunities in achieving a healthy WorkLife Balance. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and develop strategies to support your overall well-being.

**1. How often do you feel overwhelmed by work-related tasks and responsibilities, impacting your personal life?**

a) Frequently (more than 3 times a week)
b) Occasionally (1-2 times a week)
c) Rarely (less than 1 time a week)
d) Never

**2. What are the most common activities you do outside of work to recharge and relax? (Select all that apply)**

a) Exercise/Sports
b) Reading/Hobbies
c) Spending time with family/friends
d) Meditation/Yoga
e) Other (please specify)

**3. How do you prioritize your personal time and energy?**

a) I prioritize my personal life and make time for self-care
b) I try to balance my work and personal life, but sometimes one suffers
c) I prioritize my work and sacrifice personal time and energy
d) I don't prioritize my personal life, as work is my main focus

**4. Have you experienced any negative impacts on your physical or mental health due to work-related stress or long hours?**

a) Yes, I have experienced negative impacts
b) No, I have not experienced negative impacts
c) Maybe, I'm not sure

**5. How often do you take breaks or time off during the workday to recharge?**

a) Daily
b) Weekly
c) Rarely
d) Never

**6. What would you need to achieve a better WorkLife Balance, if anything? (Open-ended question)**

**7. On a scale of 1-5, how satisfied are you with your current WorkLife Balance?**

a) 1 (very dissatisfied)
b) 2 (somewhat dissatisfied)
c) 3 (neutral)
d) 4 (somewhat satisfied)
e) 5 (very satisfied)

Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts and experiences! Your input is invaluable in helping us create a more supportive and balanced work environment.

Here is a questionnaire on Workload Management with 7 questions:

**Workload Management Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We are interested in understanding how you manage your workload and how it affects your productivity and job satisfaction. Your responses will help us identify areas for improvement and implement changes to support your success.

**1. How would you rate your current workload in terms of complexity and volume?**

a) Very manageable - I can easily complete all tasks on time
b) Manageable - I need to prioritize tasks, but I can still complete them on time
c) Challenging - I need to work extra hours or adjust my priorities to meet deadlines
d) Overwhelming - I struggle to complete tasks on time, and my workload is impacting my well-being

**2. What strategies do you use to manage your workload effectively? (Select all that apply)**

a) Prioritize tasks based on urgency and importance
b) Break down large tasks into smaller, manageable chunks
c) Delegate tasks to colleagues or subordinates
d) Use project management tools or software to stay organized
e) Other (please specify)

**3. How often do you experience workload-related stress or burnout?**

a) Rarely - I'm able to manage my workload without feeling stressed
b) Occasionally - I experience stress or burnout a few times a year
c) Frequently - I experience stress or burnout regularly
d) Almost always - I'm constantly feeling stressed or burned out

**4. What are the most common obstacles you face when trying to manage your workload? (Select all that apply)**

a) Lack of resources or support
b) Unclear expectations or priorities
c) Insufficient time or unrealistic deadlines
d) Distractions or interruptions
e) Other (please specify)

**5. How do you handle changes in your workload or unexpected tasks?**

a) I adjust my priorities and focus on the new task
b) I try to complete the new task while still meeting existing deadlines
c) I ask for clarification or guidance on the new task
d) I seek help from colleagues or supervisors
e) Other (please specify)

**6. What would you like to see changed or improved in terms of workload management within our organization?**

(Open-ended question for respondents to provide their suggestions)

**7. How confident are you in your ability to manage your workload effectively?**

a) Very confident - I'm able to manage my workload without issues
b) Somewhat confident - I'm able to manage my workload with some effort
c) Not very confident - I struggle to manage my workload
d) Not at all confident - I feel overwhelmed and uncertain

Thank you for taking the time to complete this questionnaire! Your feedback is invaluable in helping us improve our workload management practices.

**Workplace Environment Questionnaire**

**Question 1:** How would you rate the overall cleanliness and organization of your workspace?

**Workplace Environment Questionnaire**

**Introduction:** We value your opinion and want to understand your experiences and perceptions of our workplace environment. Your feedback will help us identify areas for improvement and create a more comfortable and productive work environment for everyone.

**1. How would you rate the overall comfort and cleanliness of your workspace?**

a) Very comfortable and clean

c) Neutral
d) Somewhat uncomfortable and dirty
e) Very uncomfortable and dirty

a) Yes, it's very well-organized
b) Somewhat well-organized, but could be improved
c) Neutral
d) Not very well-organized
e) Not at all well-organized

**3. How would you rate the noise level in your workspace?**

a) Very quiet
b) Somewhat quiet
c) Neutral
d) Somewhat noisy
e) Very noisy

**4. Do you have a designated area for taking breaks or relaxing?**

a) Yes, and it's well-maintained
b) Yes, but it could be improved
c) No, but I wish there was one
d) No, and I don't really need one

**5. How would you rate the availability and quality of amenities such as food, water, and restrooms?**

a) Excellent
b) Good
c) Fair
d) Poor
e) Very poor

**6. Do you feel that your workspace is well-lit and visually appealing?**

a) Yes, it's very well-lit and visually appealing
b) Somewhat well-lit and visually appealing
c) Neutral
d) Not very well-lit and visually appealing
e) Not at all well-lit and visually appealing

**7. Are there any specific changes you would like to see made to our workplace environment to improve your overall experience?**
